***каторга.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каторга.html>ка́торга</a> (10695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κάτεργον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kátergon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">galley; penal labor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κάτεργος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kátergos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каторга.html>ка́торга</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kátorga</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каторга.html>ка́торги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каторга.html>ка́торги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каторга.html>ка́торг</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каторжный.html>ка́торжный</a> (17612)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каторга.html>ка́торга</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kátorga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каторжный.html>ка́торжный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kátoržnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>penal, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> convict

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каторжный.html>ка́торжная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьма́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kátoržnaja</b> tjurʹmá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">convict prison</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unbearable, very hard, backbreaking
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каторжный.html>ка́торжный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>труд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kátoržnyj</b> trud</i> ― <span class="e-translation">drudgery</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катюша.html>катю́ша</a> (10433)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катюша.html>катю́ша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Katjúša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>ка́тя</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Kátja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Katya</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, in turn diminutive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">екатери́на</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Jekaterína</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Katherine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катящий.html>катя́щий</a> (1654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кафедра.html>ка́федра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">káfedra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́льный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-álʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> church</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cathedral

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>фед<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра́ль<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

***качать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a> (3962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kačati</i>, iterative-durative for <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kotiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kačátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покачать.html>покача́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качнуть.html>качну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rock, to swing, to shake, to wobble; to dandle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:колыбель.html>колыбе́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kačátʹ</b> kolybélʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rock the cradle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kačátʹ</b> golovój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shake one's head</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pump</li>
<li>to toss, to roll, to pitch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lódku <b>kačájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the boat is tossing / rolling</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>kačálo</b> iz storoný v stóronu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was reeling from side to side</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lift up, to chair <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to toss someone up, like a group of fans their champion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to download
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скачать.html>скача́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skačátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ска́чивать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skáčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to train/pump muscle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>in the expression</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kačátʹ</b> pravá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to (persistеntly) stand up for one's rights</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kačátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качаться.html>кача́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kačátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качнуться.html>качну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rock, to swing</li>
<li>to stagger, to lurch, to reel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to oscillate, to swing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pump iron</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kačátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ча́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:качнуться.html>качну́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-кач-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:качнуть.html>качну́ть</a> (9154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kačátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (or derived the other way around).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качнуть.html>качну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kačnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rock, to swing, to shake, to wobble; to dandle (once)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:качнуть.html>качну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:колыбель.html>колыбе́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kačnútʹ</b> kolybélʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rock the cradle (once)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:качнуть.html>качну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kačnútʹ</b> golovój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shake one's head (once)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pump (once)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive or impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to toss, to roll, to pitch (once)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:качнуть.html>качну́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lódku <b>kačnúlo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the boat tossed / rolled (once)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lift up, to chair <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to toss someone up, like a group of fans their champion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to train/pump muscle (once)</li></ol>

***каша.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́ша</a> (2738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́ша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kaša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kaša</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">kaša</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">kaša</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́ша</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">káša</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́ши</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́ш</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>porridge, gruel</li>
<li>mash, mush</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> muddle, mess, confusion (e.g. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́ша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голове́</a></i>)</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кашлянуть.html>ка́шлянуть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3a③.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:кашлять.html>ка́шлять</a>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kašьľati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cough</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kašьľь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cough</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*kāˀsulia</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*kāˀslia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷeh₂s-</i>.

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chestnut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каштановый.html>кашта́новая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:роща.html>ро́ща</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kaštánovaja</b> róšča</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>chestnut</b> grove</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>chestnut-colored, maroon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каштановый.html>кашта́новые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kaštánovyje</b> vólosy</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>chestnut-colored/brown</b> hair</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
